< review>
Spoiled as I remember how Whole Foods use to be. Now even the food bar closes early, was 9;30, then 9:15, now back to 8:30, and now stocked with broad selection of fattier heavy carb foods. Prepared foods as alternative, shelves empty at 8;30 pm.This was a great store that catered to locals with good healthy selections and stocked shelves. Now since "new" corporate took over they are constantly running out of items, with vacant shelves and the selection of items has diminished. Prices have gone up, I can get some of the same foods cheaper in Maui. Milk that use to be in landfill friendly containers has now reverted to non-environment friendly plastic and the freshness date is now "Drastically" reduced compared to other Organics. The staff remain excellent and apologetic.< /review>

<Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
Like any Whole Foods this is on the high end of grocery stores in terms of prices. They have more exotic and organic ingredients. The quality is generally good and there is a massive selection of almost everything. The store itself has a rather chaotic layout. Its difficult to find what you need unless you've been there before and its usually quite crowded. That said if you just need something very specific and you don't paying a little more its a good place to grocery shop. Surprisingly they have a fairly decent craft beer selection as well.< /Review>
